The event "Diwali" will be open on November 1, 2024 at All Day.
Here's some informatino of  "Diwali".    The festival of lights, which typically lasts five days and symbolizes the spiritual “victory of light over darkness, good over evil and knowledge over ignorance.” The Hindu, Sikh and Jain traditions all honor Diwali, each tradition with its own understanding of the meaning. The event "Hanukkah" will be open on Dec. 25 - Jan. 2, 2025 at All Day.
Here's some informatino of  "Hanukkah".    Also known as the Festival of Lights, Hanukkah is an eight-day Jewish holiday celebrating the re-dedication of the Second Temple in Jerusalem in the second century A.D. It is often celebrated with the lighting of menorah candles, as well as traditional foods, games, and gifts. It is often celebrated with the lighting of menorah candles, as well as traditional foods, games, and gifts. Here's some informatino of  "Imbolc or St. Brigid’s Day".  Imbolc is a pagan sabbat that honors a spirit of renewal and new beginnings. There are various ways of observing the day, depending on one’s religious tradition..

The event "Ash Wednesday" will be open on March 5, 2025 at All Day.
Here's some informatino of  "Ash Wednesday".  Some Western Christians honor Ash Wednesday as the first day of Lent, which is the period of 40 days before Easter in which they may sacrifice ordinary pleasures to reflect on Christ’s sacrifice. On this day, there are special church services and participants may receive a cross of ashes marked on their foreheads. Christians may abstain from meat on this day..

Here's some informatino of  "Holi".  On March 14, Hindus celebrate Holi, which is known as the Festival of Colors, Festival of Spring, and the Festival of Love. It marks the arrival of spring, the divine love of Radha Krishna, and the victory of good over evil with a celebration of color and maybe attendance at their temple. This year, CMU will hold its own celebration of Holi on April 6, the Sunday of Carnival weekend..

Many Muslims fast from both food and drink between sunrise and sunset, honor halal food guidelines when they break the fast with the iftar meal, and spend more time reading the Qu’ran and praying, either alone or at a mosque..

The event "Eid al-Fitr" will be open on March 30 - 31, 2025 at All Day.
Here's some informatino of  "Eid al-Fitr".  On Eid al-Fitr, Muslims gather to celebrate the festival of breaking the Ramadan fast by praying to Allah, sharing presents, and feasting with friends and relatives. The celebration begins at sundown, the evening before the appointed day. The March 30 or 31 date is approximate, with the final date determined by the sight of the moon..

The event "Ram Navami" will be open on April 6, 2025 at All Day.
Here's some informatino of  "Ram Navami".  Ram Navami, which occurs on April 5, celebrates the birth of Lord Rama. To honor this day, Hindus clean and decorate their houses with fruits and flowers. They put an image of Rama as a baby in a cradle, and at midday, they remove the cover of the cradle and feed a special food (called Prasad) to him..

The event "Day of Silence" will be open on April 11, 2025 at All Day.
Here's some informatino of  "Day of Silence".  The Day of Silence is a student-led national event to highlight the silencing and erasure of LGBTQ+ people. Participants take a vow of silence for the day, which ends with a Breaking the Silence rally to speak about their experiences and raise awareness of ways that schools and communities can be more inclusive..

The event "Passover" will be open on April 12 - 20, 2025 at All Day.
Here's some informatino of  "Passover".  Passover (or Pesach, in Hebrew) is celebrated in remembrance of the Israelites being freed from slavery in ancient Egypt and lasts from April 12-20 this year. Beginning at sundown the night before, rituals include telling the story, fasting from leavened bread, and participating in family seder meals. Many Jews keep kosher food restrictions during this festival and attend additional religious services..

Here's some informatino of  "Holy Week or Passion Week".  Beginning with Palm Sunday on April 13, Eastern Orthodox Christians and some Western Christians commemorate the last week before Pascha or Easter Day with Passion Week or Holy Week. There are special worship services and observances such as prayer, fasting, and confession on multiple days, depending on the specific denomination..

The event "Vaisakhi" will be open on April 14, 2025 at All Day.
Here's some informatino of  "Vaisakhi".  Vaisakhi – which is also called Lohri, Pongal, Sankranthi, Gudi Padwa, and Varsh Pratipada – marks the birth of the Sikh faith, which occurred during the traditional harvest festival in Punjab. Sikh and Hindu celebrations of this festival day (April 14) may include visits to Gurdwaras, special decorations, and singing hymns..

Here's some informatino of  "Ridván".  Ridván is a 12-day festival which translates from Arabic to mean “paradise.” Though it lasts from April 20 - May 2, Baha’is observe the three holy days of the festival— the first, ninth, and twelfth—with community gatherings and rest from work..

Here's some informatino of  "Ridván".  Ridván is a 12-day festival which translates from Arabic to mean “paradise.” Though it lasts from April 20 - May 2, Baha’is observe the three holy days of the festival— the first, ninth, and twelfth—with community gatherings and rest from work..
The event "Yom HaShoah" will be open on April 23, 2025 at All Day.
Here's some informatino of  "Yom HaShoah".  This year, April 23 marks Yom HaShoah as the Jewish “Day of (remembrance of) the Holocaust and the Heroism,” which is honored in Israel and around the world. Some Jewish synagogues hold commemorative services or community programs that feature presentations from or about survivors..

Here's some informatino of  "Beltane".  Beltane, which means “bright fire” in Gaelic, is celebrated on May 1 and represents the beginning of summer in early Celtic traditions. Current Wiccan and Pagan practices honor Beltane by holding ceremonies that honor fertility, creativity, and rebirth, and fires are lit..
